# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="ac850-102">.NET Framework'teki eski üyeler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ac850-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ac850-103">Bu makaledeki tablolar .NET Framework 4.5 ve sonraki sürümlerinde derlemesi tarafından düzenlenen'te eski tür üyeleri listeler.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ac850-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ac850-104">Eski üyeler ve her derlemesindeki önerilen Alternatiflerle listesini görmek için aşağıdaki bağlantıları kullanın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ac850-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ac850-105">Bu konu eski türler üyeleri listesinde değil.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ac850-105">This topic doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ac850-106">Eski türler listesi için bkz: [eski türler](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ac850-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

<a name="SystemMembers"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="ac850-140">Sistem derlemelerde eski üyeler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ac850-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="ac850-141">Aşağıdaki tablolarda sistem derlemelerde eski üyeler listelenir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ac850-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ac850-142">Bu derlemeler için genel kullanılan\-amaçla .NET Framework hedefleyen uygulama geliştirme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ac850-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
